<script>


var exchURL="";
var sectURL="";
var regURL="";
var mktcapURL="";

var exch = get_querystring_value("exchange");
var markt = get_querystring_value("market");


var sect = get_querystring_value("industry");


var reg = get_querystring_value("region");
var cntry = get_querystring_value("country");
var state = get_querystring_value("state");


var mktcap = get_querystring_value("marketcap");


function updateURL(anchor, paramlabel, paramvalue)
{
	//remove "all" parameters from querystring
	url = document.location.href.replace(/\?\S+=ALL$|&\S+=ALL/g,"").replace(/\?\S+=ALL&/,"?");

	//remove current paramlabel if one exists
	switch(paramlabel)
	{
		case "exchange":
			if(exch!=false)
				url = url.replace("exchange="+exch,"");
			if(markt!=false)
				url = url.replace("market="+markt,"");
			url = url.replace(/&{2,}/,"&").replace("?&","?").replace(/&$/,"").replace(/\?$/,"").replace("#","");
			break;

		case "region":
			if(reg!=false)
				url = url.replace("region="+reg,"");
			if(cntry!=false)
				url = url.replace("country="+cntry,"");
			if(state!=false)
				url = url.replace("state="+state,"");
			url = url.replace(/&{2,}/,"&").replace("?&","?").replace(/&$/,"").replace(/\?$/,"").replace("#","");
			break;

		case "industry":
			if(sect!=false)
				url = url.replace("industry="+sect,"").replace(/&{2,}/,"&").replace("?&","?").replace(/&$/,"").replace(/\?$/,"").replace("#","");
			break;

		case "marketcap":
			if(mktcap!=false)
				url = url.replace("marketcap="+mktcap,"").replace(/&{2,}/,"&").replace("?&","?").replace(/&$/,"").replace(/\?$/,"").replace("#","");
			break;

	}
	url = url+"&"+paramlabel+"="+paramvalue;
	url = url.replace(".aspx&",".aspx?").replace("?&","?");
	anchor.href = url;
}

	
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var curlist;
var hl;
var ref;
var startIndex;
var endIndex;
var result;
if(exch!=false && exch!= "ALL")
{
	curlist = document.getElementById("exchangeshowall").getElementsByTagName('a');
	for(i=0;i<curlist.length;i++)
	{
		hl = curlist[i].attributes.getNamedItem('href');
		ref = hl.nodeValue;
		startIndex = ref.indexOf("exchange=")+9;
		endIndex = ref.indexOf("&",startIndex);
		if(endIndex!=-1)
			result = ref.slice(startIndex,endIndex);
		else
			result = ref.slice(startIndex);
		if(result==exch)
		{
			curlist[i].className = "current";
			break;
		}
	}
}
if(reg!=false && reg!= "ALL")
{
	curlist = document.getElementById("regionshowall").getElementsByTagName('a');
	for(i=0;i<curlist.length;i++)
	{
		hl = curlist[i].attributes.getNamedItem('href');
		ref = hl.nodeValue;
		startIndex = ref.indexOf("region=")+7;
		endIndex = ref.indexOf("&",startIndex);
		if(endIndex!=-1)
			result = ref.slice(startIndex,endIndex);
		else
			result = ref.slice(startIndex);
		if(result==reg)
		{
			curlist[i].className = "current";
			break;
		}
	}
}
if(sect!=false && sect!= "ALL")
{
	curlist = document.getElementById("industryshowall").getElementsByTagName('a');
	for(i=0;i<curlist.length;i++)
	{
		hl = curlist[i].attributes.getNamedItem('href');
		ref = hl.nodeValue;
		startIndex = ref.indexOf("industry=")+9;
		endIndex = ref.indexOf("&",startIndex);
		if(endIndex!=-1)
			result = ref.slice(startIndex,endIndex);
		else
			result = ref.slice(startIndex);
		if(result==sect)
		{
			curlist[i].className = "current";
			break;
		}
	}
}
if(mktcap!=false && mktcap!="ALL")
{
	curlist = document.getElementById("marketcapshowall").getElementsByTagName('a');
	for(i=0;i<curlist.length;i++)
	{
		hl = curlist[i].attributes.getNamedItem('href');
		ref = hl.nodeValue.replace(/\+/g," ");
		startIndex = ref.indexOf("marketcap=")+10;
		endIndex = ref.indexOf("&",startIndex);
		if(endIndex!=-1)
			result = ref.slice(startIndex,endIndex);
		else
			result = ref.slice(startIndex);
		if(result==mktcap)
		{
			curlist[i].className = "current";
			break;
		}
	}
}
		
</script>

<script>


var exchURL="";
var sectURL="";
var regURL="";
var mktcapURL="";

var exch = get_querystring_value("exchange");
var markt = get_querystring_value("market");


var sect = get_querystring_value("industry");


var reg = get_querystring_value("region");
var cntry = get_querystring_value("country");
var state = get_querystring_value("state");


var mktcap = get_querystring_value("marketcap");


function updateURL(anchor, paramlabel, paramvalue)
{
	//remove "all" parameters from querystring
	url = document.location.href.replace(/\?\S+=ALL$|&\S+=ALL/g,"").replace(/\?\S+=ALL&/,"?");

	//remove current paramlabel if one exists
	switch(paramlabel)
	{
		case "exchange":
			if(exch!=false)
				url = url.replace("exchange="+exch,"");
			if(markt!=false)
				url = url.replace("market="+markt,"");
			url = url.replace(/&{2,}/,"&").replace("?&","?").replace(/&$/,"").replace(/\?$/,"").replace("#","");
			break;

		case "region":
			if(reg!=false)
				url = url.replace("region="+reg,"");
			if(cntry!=false)
				url = url.replace("country="+cntry,"");
			if(state!=false)
				url = url.replace("state="+state,"");
			url = url.replace(/&{2,}/,"&").replace("?&","?").replace(/&$/,"").replace(/\?$/,"").replace("#","");
			break;

		case "industry":
			if(sect!=false)
				url = url.replace("industry="+sect,"").replace(/&{2,}/,"&").replace("?&","?").replace(/&$/,"").replace(/\?$/,"").replace("#","");
			break;

		case "marketcap":
			if(mktcap!=false)
				url = url.replace("marketcap="+mktcap,"").replace(/&{2,}/,"&").replace("?&","?").replace(/&$/,"").replace(/\?$/,"").replace("#","");
			break;

	}
	url = url+"&"+paramlabel+"="+paramvalue;
	url = url.replace(".aspx&",".aspx?").replace("?&","?");
	anchor.href = url;
}

	
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var curlist;
var hl;
var ref;
var startIndex;
var endIndex;
var result;
if(exch!=false && exch!= "ALL")
{
	curlist = document.getElementById("exchangeshowall").getElementsByTagName('a');
	for(i=0;i<curlist.length;i++)
	{
		hl = curlist[i].attributes.getNamedItem('href');
		ref = hl.nodeValue;
		startIndex = ref.indexOf("exchange=")+9;
		endIndex = ref.indexOf("&",startIndex);
		if(endIndex!=-1)
			result = ref.slice(startIndex,endIndex);
		else
			result = ref.slice(startIndex);
		if(result==exch)
		{
			curlist[i].className = "current";
			break;
		}
	}
}
if(reg!=false && reg!= "ALL")
{
	curlist = document.getElementById("regionshowall").getElementsByTagName('a');
	for(i=0;i<curlist.length;i++)
	{
		hl = curlist[i].attributes.getNamedItem('href');
		ref = hl.nodeValue;
		startIndex = ref.indexOf("region=")+7;
		endIndex = ref.indexOf("&",startIndex);
		if(endIndex!=-1)
			result = ref.slice(startIndex,endIndex);
		else
			result = ref.slice(startIndex);
		if(result==reg)
		{
			curlist[i].className = "current";
			break;
		}
	}
}
if(sect!=false && sect!= "ALL")
{
	curlist = document.getElementById("industryshowall").getElementsByTagName('a');
	for(i=0;i<curlist.length;i++)
	{
		hl = curlist[i].attributes.getNamedItem('href');
		ref = hl.nodeValue;
		startIndex = ref.indexOf("industry=")+9;
		endIndex = ref.indexOf("&",startIndex);
		if(endIndex!=-1)
			result = ref.slice(startIndex,endIndex);
		else
			result = ref.slice(startIndex);
		if(result==sect)
		{
			curlist[i].className = "current";
			break;
		}
	}
}
if(mktcap!=false && mktcap!="ALL")
{
	curlist = document.getElementById("marketcapshowall").getElementsByTagName('a');
	for(i=0;i<curlist.length;i++)
	{
		hl = curlist[i].attributes.getNamedItem('href');
		ref = hl.nodeValue.replace(/\+/g," ");
		startIndex = ref.indexOf("marketcap=")+10;
		endIndex = ref.indexOf("&",startIndex);
		if(endIndex!=-1)
			result = ref.slice(startIndex,endIndex);
		else
			result = ref.slice(startIndex);
		if(result==mktcap)
		{
			curlist[i].className = "current";
			break;
		}
	}
}
